commit accca801b564abd0b57997035739ca0a0a5a09a2
Author: Thomas Bachman <tbachman@yahoo.com>
Date:   Tue Nov 18 12:55:15 2025 +0000

    Add opflex connection monitoring script
    
    The opflex agent has encountered corner cases during switch reboots,
    which cause the agent to stop attempting to reconnect to the fabric.
    This patch adds a script that monitors for connections to the opflex
    TCP port, and if no connections are detected for a continued period
    of time, it writes to the reset.conf file, triggering the reconnect
    process.
    
    (cherry picked from commit f79bd8cf0aa0f5fd48e65e0f221582a5555c7c66)

+EXPECTED_TAG_PREFIX=6.1.1.5
+[[ 6.1.1.5 != \6\.\1\.\1\.\5* ]]

++grep 'Created by Travis Job'
+tag_message=
+[[ ! -z '' ]]

    Add opflex connection monitoring script
    
    The opflex agent has encountered corner cases during switch reboots,
    which cause the agent to stop attempting to reconnect to the fabric.
    This patch adds a script that monitors for connections to the opflex
    TCP port, and if no connections are detected for a continued period
    of time, it writes to the reset.conf file, triggering the reconnect
    process.
    
    (cherry picked from commit f79bd8cf0aa0f5fd48e65e0f221582a5555c7c66)
